1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the sixteen digit representation of Chinese graphic characters and binary code for information technology 。	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document is applicable to the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output of information in Chinese and other text-graphic characters.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document is intended for the technical categories of products with information processing and exchange capabilities for Chinese and other text-graphic characters, including but not limited to software products represented by input methods, optical character recognition (OCR), editing, correction, machine translation, speech synthesis, transcription, and joinery, and notebook products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book readers, and learning machines.	no

4 字汇	4 The Word	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Summary of the project	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters in this file are encoded in single, double, or quad-byte encodings.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte portion contains all 128 characters from GB/T 11383 I 1989 0x00 to 0x7F 。	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 The two-byte part	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The two-byte part contains all the graphic characters in GB/T 2312 a 1980 and the CJK Unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000 as well as some graphic characters ▽.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The characters in the two-byte section are as specified in Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	The graphics, code location and function of the semantic descriptor shall be in accordance with the provisions of Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 Uniform Code for Chinese characters used in China, Japan, the People's Republic of China, and Vietnam.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Characters with unique abstract characters are assigned a separate code position; characters with the same abstract characters from different sources are assigned a common code position.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The encoded characters are called CJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK stands for China, Japan, and Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Quad byte part	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte section contains 66 of the CJK Unicode characters from GB/T 13000 in addition to the above two-byte characters ((9FA6 and 9FEF, excluding the 8 characters from 9FB4 to 9FBB), CJK Unicode Extension A, CJK Unicode Extension BCJK Unicode Extension C, CJK Unicode Extension DCJK Unicode Extension CJK Unicode Extension F and the characters of the minority characters already encoded in GB/Manufacturer 13000	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The characters in the four-byte section are as defined in Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 General structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the English language, all numbers with 0x are represented in the decimal system, whereas those without 0x are represented in the hexadecimal system.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	The encoded digits in the appendix are represented in the decimal system, while the other digits are represented in the hexadecimal system.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte portion uses the encoding structure of GB/T 11383 I 1989, so that the 0x00 to 0x7F bytes are used.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The binary digits are represented by two eight-digit binary bit strings, starting with 0x81 and 0xFE, followed by 0x40 and 0x7E and 0x80 and 0xFE respectively.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte part is used in GB/Work 11383 1 1989 Not used 0x30 1 0x39 As a suffix to the two-byte extension, the encoding range is 0x81308130 1 0xFE39FE39 。	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The first four-byte character is encoded as 0x81 by 0xFE; the second is encoded as 0x30 by 0x39; the third is encoded as 0x81 by 0xFE; the fourth is encoded as 0x30 by 0x39 。 i.e.: 0x813081301 by 0x81308139; 0x813082301 by 0x81308239 by 0x8130FEFE301 by 0x8130FE39 ; 0x813181301 by 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c 0URo23061393 by 0xFE39301 by 0xFE3939 。	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and berth allocation are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1 ◦.	no

自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	The 1058400 bytes from 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39 are used for the 16 auxiliary planes corresponding to GB/T 13000, and the character order is exactly the same as the corresponding bytes in GB/I 13000's 16 auxiliary planes.	no

If we find that the content of the manual page is causing obvious confusion and complaints due to its obsolescence, we stop publishing it. 描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION C and C++ compilers are integrated. They all handle input files in one or more of four steps: preprocessing, compilation, assembly, and linking.	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The source file suffix identifies the language of the source file, but for the compiler, the suffix name controls the default setting:	yes

在连接阶段中,所有对应于源程序的.e 文件，-1 库文件, 无法识别的文件名(包括指定的.o H 标文件和 .a 库文件)按命令行中的顺序传递给连接器选项 (OPTIONS)	At the connection stage, all corresponding.e files, -1 library files, unidentified file names ((including the specified.o H flag files and.a library files) are passed to the connector options in order from the command line	no
选项必须分立给出 : de ' 完全不同于 `-d -r '.	The option must be given separately: de'is completely different from `-d-r '.	no
大多数 ` -=E :和 `-W' 选项有两个相反的格式 : -fname 和 -fno-name (或 -Wname 和 -Wno- name).	Most ` -=E: and `-W' options have two opposite formats: -fname and -fno-name (or -Wname and -Wno-name).	no

这个选项应用于后面所有的输入文件, 直到遇着下一个 `-x' 选项 .language 的可选	This option applies to all subsequent input files until the next `-x' option is encountered.	yes

如果只操作四个阶段( 预处理, 编译, 汇编, 连接)中的一部分, 可以使用 ` -x' 选项 (或文件名后 Ah) 告诉 geo 从哪里开始,用 `~-c' ，`-s' ,或 `-E' 选项告诉 geo 到哪里结束.注意,某些选项组合 (例如 ，`-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c 编译或汇编源文件, ETER. ERA ATI 缺省情况下， GCC 通过用 ` .o' 蔡换源文件名后级 ` .ec 标文件名. 可以使用-o 选项选择其他名字.GCC忽略 -ec 选项后面任何无法识别的输入文伯 -S F 何事情.	If only a portion of the four stages (Preprocess, Compile, Compile, Connect) is operated, the ` -x' option (or Ah after the filename) can be used to tell geo where to start, and the `~-c', `-s', or `-E' option to tell geo where to end. Note that some combinations of options (e.g., `-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c compile or compile source files, ETER. In the absence of ERA ATI, GCC is used by `.o' to replace the source file name with the post-level `.ec filename. Other options can be used to choose the name.	yes
了的目标文件.	The targeted files.	yes
编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	The compilation is stopped and no compilation is done.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	The compiler for GNU does not have this problem, since the compilers for those systems cannot read data from the pipeline, and the compiler is able to accept the C "dialect": support for C programs that conform to the ANSI standard.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This turns off certain keywords in GNU Cc that are incompatible with ANSI Cc, as well as ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax that are indicated as acceptable and rarely used, and disables them despite the fact that they are used in all standard libraries. The main function returns an int value, typical of almost all programs except the kernel.	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	For function declarations without parameters, such as `int foo ();', C-style handling --- i.e. no indication of the number or type of parameters. (Only for C++).	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Normally, a function like foo would mean that the argument is empty in C++.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The section lists here are removed to try to support some aspects of the traditional C compiler.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	We have removed the details so that when the content is out of date, people won't be able to HERI it.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for c++ programs (not C), the '∀ -traditional' option brings an additional effect, allowing this to be assigned.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	The result of this is the same as the result of the '`-Ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp attempts to support some aspects of the traditional Cc preprocessor.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	In particular, the preprocessor mentioned above, but not including the other effects of the '`-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows the use of the character `$' in identifiers (C++ only).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the option '∀-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' to explicitly prohibit the use of the '∀$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the `$' character by default on some target systems, but not all.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv allows implicit conversion of the ant type to the enumeration type (MEF c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	In normal circumstances, GNU C++ allows the conversion from enum to int, but not vice versa.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal-templates generates a smaller code (limited to c++) for the template declaration, by generating a copy of each template function only where they are defined.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To successfully use this option, you must mark `#pragma implementatio' (definition) or `#Pragma interface' (declaration) in all files that use the template.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When a program compiles with `-fexternal-templates', all template instantiations are external types. You must have the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be done through typedef, which cites each instance as needed.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondingly, if the default option ` -fno-exteznal-templates' is used when compiling, all template instances are explicitly set to built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except the constructor subfunction and the mnew or delete member operator) are treated as virtual functions of the class in which they are located.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not imply that every call to a member function will pass through the internal null table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can determine that a virtual function can be called directly; this is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch Allows type mismatch of the second and third parameters of a conditional expression.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of this expression is Void.-fthis-is-variable allowing this to be assigned (only for c++).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	The incorporation of user-customized free storage management mechanisms into c++ makes the attributable '`this' seem out of date.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, this assignment is invalid inside the class member function.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backwards compatibility, you can enable this by using the '`-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char Defines char as a symbolless type, like unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Each machine has its own default char type. It can be either an unsigned char or a signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz when relying on the symbolic nature of the data.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written using only simple char, and the terminal block is either symmetrical (or symmetricalless, depending on the target machine that wrote the program).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its antiderivative, allows the program to work on the corresponding default.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be clearly defined as a signed char or an unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly like one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If there is no explicit declaration of the ` signed' or "unsigned' modifier, these options are used to define a bitfield with or without a symbol.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bit fields are signed because the basic integer types they inherit, such as int, are signed, however, if the '`-traditional' option is specified, the bit fields are always unsigned.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings stores string constants in a writable data segment, and does not give it special treatment.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is to make it compatible with some older programs, which are thinking that changing the string constant is a very bad idea, and the '`-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Summary of the execution	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	The impact of coronavirus on the drug market	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact could be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global outbreak of coronavirus pneumonia has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has left healthcare systems in a state of near collapse, and restrictive measures imposed by governments have caused severe disruption in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	The impact of the epidemic on the drug market is unclear and difficult to predict, but it could have far-reaching consequences.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs, as restrictions on movement also limit access to precursors and basic chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers who cannot cross the border due to travel restrictions may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	The patterns of drug use and supply may change, and the government's ability to respond may be hindered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The transformation of the coronavirus is unprecedented, but there are lessons to be learned from past crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some users began to look for cheaper synthetic substances and shifted their patterns of use to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments have cut budgets related to drugs.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	Interventions such as prevention of drug use and related risk behaviors and drug treatment services could be hit hard if governments respond to the current economic downturn in the same way.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, the priority of interception operations and international cooperation may be reduced, making it easier for traffickers to act.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	The report also highlights the fact that the number of countries where drugs are smuggled via commercial airlines is high, and that these countries are expected to be the most directly affected by the drug trafficking activity.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Consumers have been known to carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in their backpacks or hidden in their personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. Due to restrictions on air passenger transportation in almost all places, the supply of drugs using commercial air travel may be completely interrupted.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	Although the international postal supply chain is also affected, the use of darknet and cargo mail for trafficking activities may increase.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the economic recession and related closures could disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	Due to rising unemployment and lack of opportunities, poor and vulnerable people will be more likely to use drugs in harmful ways, to develop drug addiction disorders, and to turn to illicit activities related to drugs, whether in production or transportation.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	The drug trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation to provide services to vulnerable populations and recruit new members to strengthen their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	These changes could quickly take root and become a new reality in many communities as the government's ability to respond declines.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and complexity	no
市场增长	Growth of the market	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	Population growth patterns partly explain why the market is expanding	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug use has been increasing in all parts of the world, both in terms of overall numbers and in terms of the proportion of drug users in the world's population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009, an estimated 210 million people used drugs, or 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, compared to an estimated 269 million in 2018, or 5.3% of the population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	Over the past two decades, drug use in developing countries has increased much faster than in developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This reflects to some extent the difference in overall population growth over this period, with 7% in developed countries and 28% in developing countries, but also the faster growth of the young population in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	The largest proportion of drug users are adolescents and young adults.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	Between 2000 and 2018, the population of this age group in developing countries increased by 16%, while the population of this age group in developed countries decreased by 10%.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization is a driver of current and future drug markets	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	In both developed and developing countries, drug use is more prevalent in urban areas than in rural areas.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	The overall increase in drug use is partly due to the massive migration of people from rural to urban areas, where more than half of the world's population now lives, compared to 34% in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization may be a key factor in the future dynamics of the drug market, especially in developing countries where urbanization trends are more prominent.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increasing wealth is associated with an increase in drug use, but the burden of disease is greatest among the poorest people in the world, and drug use is more prevalent in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	The drug is also linked to the richest parts of the world, where it is used in the production of drugs such as cocaine.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	In the same way, the prevalence of drug use is higher among the wealthy in different countries.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, the highest rates of drug addiction are found in people with lower socioeconomic status.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a small number of countries show a link between harmful patterns of drug use, disease and low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns seem less common in the wealthier social classes.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global coronavirus pneumonia crisis are likely to increase the risk for the most vulnerable groups, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been linked in the past to an increase in drug use, an epidemic that has already forced tens of millions of people around the world out of work.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	The pandemic of coronavirus pneumonia could lead to more farmers or illegal crop cultivation, or because of the reduced control capacity of the state authorities, or because more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities under the economic crisis.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	The associated restrictions on coronavirus pneumonia have led to a reduction in air and land traffic, which may have increased maritime trafficking, with a lower risk of interception at sea and more trafficking than by air or land.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	Recently, there have been reports of cocaine being shipped directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The emergence of non-internationally controlled substances is stable, but the market for potentially harmful new opioids is growing and becoming more complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant-based substances such as cannabis, cocaine and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. Non-medical use of drugs is also growing rapidly.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	The domestic market of the Member States is home to approximately 500 new active substances per year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Currently, the majority of these are stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor activators and a small number of opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	Although the overall number of new psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportion has changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	Opioid-like new psychoactive substances accounted for only 2% of the total number of new psychoactive substance categories identified in 2014, but this figure rose to 9% by 2018 [2].	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the newer psychoactive substances, such as opioids, are analogues of fentanyl, whose medicinal effects and harms have been demonstrated to cause overdose deaths in North America and other regions, but to a lesser degree.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, fentanyl is used as a hallucinogen for heroin and other drugs (including cocaine and methamphetamine), and in the manufacture of counterfeit medicinal opiates.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	Some evidence suggests that injection of new psychoactive substances (NPS) is also a phenomenon in Europe: a study of discarded syringe residues in six European cities found that many syringes were laced with the new psychoactive substance, mercury, which produces an exciting effect	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 The use of new psychoactive substances may become more entrenched in vulnerable groups	no

有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries reported the use of new psychoactive substances in prisons, with the majority of countries identifying synthetic cannabis as the main challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	The regulation of precursor chemicals has forced drug makers to innovate, and many of the chemicals most commonly used as precursors to synthesize drugs such as ketamine, methylamine and methamphetamine have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug dealers and manufacturers have been looking for alternatives to not only loosely regulated substances, but also chemicals specifically designed to circumvent regulation, the so-called "special-purpose" precursors.	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at preventing the spread of novel coronavirus pneumonia are likely to further squeeze out poisoners who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico suggests that this is already a reality: in March 2020, it was reported that a shortage of methylamine precursors imported from East Asia had led to higher prices in Mexico and the United States.	no

政策变化和变化趋势	Policy changes and trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most jurisdictions that have legalized non-medical use of cannabis have seen an increase in its use.	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	The manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use is permitted in 11 jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay and the United States.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of these jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized non-medical use of cannabis.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In the first two states to pass legislation, Colorado and Washington, non-medical use of marijuana by adults has increased, especially in the past month, and daily or near-daily use has exceeded the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show that the use of cannabis in Uruguay has increased since 2011, with the use almost doubling last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This suggests that the main reason for the increase is the frequent and frequent use of cannabis.	yes

然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, in 2019, 40% of cannabis users still obtained some products from illegal sources.	yes

相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In comparison, seizures in the rest of the world nearly doubled during the same period. The pattern of seizures suggests that policies aimed at opening up the cannabis market played a key role in the decline.	no

弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	The harm of legal and illegal drug markets to vulnerable groups The availability of opioids, medicinal drugs used for pain management and palliative care, is unevenly distributed across regions, mainly in high-income countries.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, more than 90% of all medicinal opioids available for medical use were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% of the world's population lives in North America, 40% in Europe, and 2% in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	These countries account for about 12% of the world's population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that 88% of the world's population lives in low- and middle-income countries, but less than 10% of the world's population consumes medicinal opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to access to prescription opioids are related to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems, and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing drug-related diseases, with 35.6 million people suffering from drug-related diseases in 2018.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education and social marginalization may increase the risk of drug use disorders and exacerbate their consequences. Research in high-income countries confirms this, and in these studies, the socioeconomic trajectories of individuals that are disadvantaged are associated with the risk of drug use disorders, not just their situation at a particular point in time.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug use disorders also exacerbate socioeconomic disadvantages, further increasing the risk of unemployment, poverty and homelessness, thus contributing to the vicious cycle of disadvantage. These outcomes may also be related to the stigmatizing attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, minorities and migrants, diverse groups of sexual orientation, people displaced by armed conflict or disaster, and people in rural settings may also be disproportionately affected by drug-related illnesses or have problems accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	The last decade has seen an increase in the impact of harmful drug use on wider society, according to the Disability Adjusted Life Years (DALY) indicator, which estimates the number of years of healthy life lost due to disability and premature death.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	The global disability-adjusted life expectancy attributed to drug use increased by 17% between 2007 and 2018.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The disability-adjusted life years associated with liver cancer caused by untreated hepatitis C, common among injection drug users, are particularly high, with a 40% increase.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is complex and it is difficult to determine all the causal relationships between the use of psychoactive substances and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited data from around the world suggests that binge drinking may be a significant factor in deaths.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But alcohol seems to be more important than drugs in violence.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	While drug use may lead to crime, in some cases this link can be attributed in part to a variety of intermediate factors, such as socioeconomic disadvantage and other types of adversity caused by personal risk, family environment and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is multifaceted.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	Where there is a stable criminal structure, large-scale organized crime, including international drug trafficking, is likely to be carried out in a non-violent manner.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the presence and extent of violence depends less on the volume of trafficking than on certain changes that destabilize the balance of power between organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of the illegal market, the death or incarceration of known criminals, and law enforcement measures that weaken one group over another.	no

据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	It is estimated that in 2018, there were 189 million people who used cannabis, making it the most used drug in the world.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	In comparison, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	The dangers of opioids are being ignored because of the low number of users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Of the estimated 167,000 deaths related to drug use disorders in 2017, 66% were caused by these substances, and 50% of the 21 million years of life lost in the United States are believed to be due to disability or premature death caused by drug use.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	Non-medical use of synthetic opioids exacerbates public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West, Central and North Africa, the opioid crisis is exacerbated by Kumamoto; in North America, it is Fentanyl. The two regions have little in common in terms of economics, demographics or general patterns of drug use, but are struggling to combat the opioid crisis fueled by the availability and low cost of the substance.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has led to an increase in opioid overdose deaths over the past 20 years.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths reported in the United States were related to fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada reports similar results, but with lower numbers.	no

在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	The market for non-medical use of quinoa has grown significantly in West, Central and North Africa.	no

使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	What makes the crisis worse is that these substances are available in both the drug and illicit markets, making it harder to detect and prevent their abuse.	no

在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine coexist, sometimes interchangeably, such that as the use of one drug increases, the use of the other drug decreases, sometimes simultaneously increasing and decreasing to meet the demands of the same market.	no

欧盟峰会为难民政策争论，欧盟官员：接收过程步步瓶颈-中新网	EU officials: Reception process is a bottleneck - China News Network	yes
欧盟峰会为难民政策争吵不休，欧盟官员：接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈	EU summits fight over refugee policy, EU officials: bottlenecks at every step of the admission process	yes
【环球时报驻比利时特派记者 牛瑞飞】据法新社2月10日报道，在当天最新的一次欧盟峰会上，欧盟委员会主席冯德莱恩表示，欧盟领导人同意就非法移民问题出台更严格的政策，以此更易于驱逐非法移民。	According to AFP, at the latest EU summit on February 10, European Commission President Jean-Claude Juncker said that EU leaders had agreed to a stricter policy on illegal immigration to make it easier to deport illegal immigrants.	yes
据报道，欧盟此举是对欧洲日益增长的非法移民问题关注的回应，如今，欧盟的核心问题在于，最终能被遣返的非法移民人数很少。	The move was reportedly a response to the EU's growing concern about illegal immigration, which is now at the heart of the EU's problem with the small number of illegal immigrants who can ultimately be returned.	yes
根据峰会文件，欧盟领导人呼吁委员会“立即调动大量欧盟资金”，以基础设施和监视等手段加强外部边界。	According to the summit documents, EU leaders called on the Commission to immediately mobilize large amounts of EU funds to strengthen the external borders, including infrastructure and surveillance.	yes
然而，欧盟与各成员国就围栏费用支付等问题争吵不休。	However, the EU and its member states are still in dispute over the payment of fencing fees and other issues.	yes
冯德莱恩一再表示，欧盟资金不会支付相关费用。	The EU funds will not cover the costs, Vanderleien has repeatedly said.	yes
但一些成员国的外交官员称，如果欧盟能分担外部边界沿线安装摄像头、瞭望塔和其他基础设施的部分，这将给各国腾出国家预算从而加快建设进程。	But diplomats from some member states say that if the EU can share the cost of installing cameras, watchtowers and other infrastructure along the external border, it will free up national budgets and speed up the construction process.	yes
欧洲Euractiv网站称，欧盟官员承认，难民接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈，有限的接收能力和成员国不堪重负的移民当局无法阻止难民在欧盟各国提交“无数”庇护申请，欧盟的难民接收系统处于近乎“永久性的危机”中。	European officials acknowledge that there are bottlenecks at every step of the refugee admission process, that limited admission capacity and overwhelmed immigration authorities in member states are unable to stop refugees from submitting a huge number of asylum applications in EU countries, and that the EU's refugee admission system is in near-permanent crisis, according to the European website Euractiv.	yes
据欧盟委员会估计，欧盟的申根国家去年收到超92万份庇护申请，比前一年增加近半。	The European Commission estimates that the EU's Schengen countries received more than 920,000 asylum applications last year, almost half as many as the previous year.	yes
与此同时，欧盟去年记录到超 33万次非法入境。	Meanwhile, the EU recorded more than 330,000 illegal entries last year.	no
在该背景下，此次峰会还就一项“原则”达成协议，即欧盟国家可根据另一个成员国的法院判决将非法移民遣返回国。	In this context, the summit also agreed on a principle of subsidiarity, whereby EU countries can return illegal migrants to their home countries based on a judgment of a court in another member state.	no
此外，报道称，欧盟领导人还同意“增加对安全国家概念的使用”，这将为欧盟制定共同清单开辟道路。	In addition, EU leaders also agreed to increase the use of the concept of safe countries, which would pave the way for the EU to develop a common list, the report said.	no

美国升级“芯片战”重创全球半导体产业-中新网	US upgrade of silicon chips hits global semiconductor industry hard - China news	yes
最近，美国对华“芯片战”大有升级之势——先是荷兰、日本两国在美国施压下，同意启动对华半导体制造设备出口的管制；后有外媒报道，美国政府正考虑切断美国供应商与华为公司之间的所有联系，禁止美国供应商向华为提供任何产品；拜登政府还准备公布一项行政命令，限制美国对敏感的中国科技行业的投资……2023年开年不久，美国在遏制中国半导体相关产业发展上就恶招不断。	Recently, the US war on Huawei chips has escalated significantly, with the Netherlands and Japan agreeing to start regulating the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China under pressure from the US. Foreign media reports have reported that the US government is considering cutting all ties between US suppliers and Huawei companies, prohibiting US suppliers from providing any products to Huawei. The Biden administration is also preparing to issue an executive order restricting US investment in the sensitive Chinese technology industry.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the United States has never stopped its efforts to combat China's silicon chip development, while cracking down on China's semiconductor supply chain, while building a semiconductor industry chain alliance to make China look like China, in an attempt to completely open up China in the advanced semiconductor industry.	yes
无论是拉拢韩国建立“技术同盟”，还是与韩国、日本和中国台湾地区建立芯片“四方联盟”，亦或借由美日印澳“四边机制”“印太经济框架”等机制建立半导体产业链“小圈子”，美国通过把政治化、阵营化、武器化的手段引入半导体产业，企图搭建美国主导的封闭产供链循环，从而弥补其在芯片制造领域的短板，维护其在全球芯片产业的优势地位。	Whether it is to establish a silicon technology alliance with South Korea, or to establish a four-party alliance with South Korea, Japan and Taiwan in China, or to establish a semiconductor industry chain link by means of the US-Japanese-Indian-Australian Quadrilateral Mechanism and the Printing Sea Economic Framework, the United States is trying to build a closed production supply chain cycle led by the United States by introducing politicization, militarization, and weaponization.	yes
然而，美国大张旗鼓的对华“芯战术”，也是“伤敌一千自损八百”。	However, the US's tactical victory over China was also a blow to the enemy's self-defense.	yes
最近，美国知名芯片制造设备供应商泛林集团宣布，受最新一轮对华芯片制造设备出口禁令影响，集团将解雇1300名全职员工，未来两个季度还计划解雇1400名临时员工。	Recently, PanLinx, a well-known chip manufacturing equipment supplier in the United States, announced that it would lay off 1,300 full-time employees and 1,400 temporary employees in the next two quarters, due to the latest round of export bans on Chinese chip manufacturing equipment.	yes
全球光刻机巨头荷兰阿斯麦控股公司最近警告，禁止向中国出口半导体制造设备，可能导致半导体价格上涨。	The global photogrammetry giant Asma Holding, a Dutch company, recently warned that a ban on the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China could lead to higher semiconductor prices.	yes
美媒分析，在美国政府对中国芯片和半导体等行业实施蛮横打压后，许多美国公司深受其害，包括电子设计自动化工具开发商、芯片设计商、晶圆制造设备生产商、芯片制造商本身等。	After the US government cracked down on industries such as chips and semiconductors in China, many US companies were hit hard, including developers of electronic design automation tools, chip designers, manufacturers of crystal manufacturing equipment, and chip manufacturers themselves.	yes
美国所谓打压中国先进半导体产业，却把全球半导体产业链、供应链拖下了水。	The US is supposedly cracking down on China's advanced semiconductor industry, but instead dragging down the global semiconductor industry and supply chain.	yes
半导体产业是高技术和知识密集型产业，早已形成联系紧密的全球半导体产业链。	The semiconductor industry is a high-tech and knowledge-intensive industry, which has long formed a tightly linked global semiconductor industry chain.	yes
据专业人士估算，基于专业化分工，半导体产品的整个生产过程需要跨越各国边境70次以上，全程达到100天。	According to experts, the entire production process of semiconductor products based on specialized division of labor requires crossing the borders of countries more than 70 times, and the entire process takes 100 days.	no
尽管美国半导体产业基础较强，但在制造能力特别是先进制程工艺上较为薄弱，严重依赖东亚地区。	Although the US semiconductor industry has a strong base, it is weak in manufacturing capacity, especially in advanced manufacturing processes, and heavily relies on East Asia.	no
即便美国极力引导先进芯片产供链转向美国主导的“小圈子”区域化发展，但全球半导体相关产业的地区分布和相互依赖局面很难被改变。	Even if the US is able to steer the advanced chip supply chain towards a US-led small-circle regionalisation, the regional distribution and interdependence of the global semiconductor industry is difficult to change.	no
美国强力“重塑”“去中国化”的半导体产业链，重创全球半导体产业。	The US is reshaping the semiconductor industry chain from China to China, creating a new global semiconductor industry.	no
芯片是全球未来产业的核心，芯片产业的发展离不开全球各国共同参与。	The chip industry is the core of the future of the global industry, and the development of the chip industry is inseparable from the participation of all countries in the world.	no
近年来，美国采取一系列单边行动，相继出台《创新与竞争法案》《2022年美国竞争法案》《芯片和科学法案》，利用科技霸权，巩固本国技术领先优势；对盟友“恩威并施”，诱逼英特尔、台积电、三星等芯片制造企业赴美设厂，极力确保美国在芯片领域的全球领导地位。	In recent years, the United States has taken a series of unilateral actions, including the introduction of the Innovation and Competition Act, the US Competition Act, the US Chip and Science Act of 2022, the use of technological hegemony to consolidate its technological leadership; the use of allied technology to lure chip manufacturers such as Intel, TSMC, and Samsung to enter the US plant, and the efforts to ensure the US's global leadership in the chip field.	no
短期看，美国确实给中国的芯片产业及相关产业发展制造了麻烦，收获了现实利益。	In the short term, the US has indeed created problems for China's chip industry and related industries, and reaped real benefits.	no
但长期看，美国歇斯底里地打压，倒逼中国芯片产业不断突破，让自己失去了巨大的中国市场，最终会极大削弱美国科技企业的创新意愿和创新能力，损害全球芯片产业发展。	But in the long run, the hysterical US pushback against China's chip industry, which has been making breakthroughs, will cost it a huge Chinese market, and ultimately weaken the innovative will and ability of US tech companies, and damage the development of the global chip industry.	no

去年11月银保监会制定了《商业银行和理财公司个人养老金业务管理暂行办法 》 。	In November last year, the Banking and Insurance Regulatory Commission (BCR) issued a temporary measure to regulate the personal pension business of commercial banks and financial institutions in Hong Kong.	no
《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The Participant's Personal Pension Fund Account is used to purchase Personal Pension Products such as Personal Pension Savings, Personal Pension Property Management, Personal Pension Insurance Products, Personal Pension Public Fund Products.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the Ministry of Social Affairs, the Ministry of Finance and the National Tax Administration issued a notice to start implementing the personal pension system in Beijing, Tianjin, and 36 pioneering cities and regions such as Shijiazhuang, Xiong'an New Area, Shanxi and Jining City in Hebei.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	As of the end of 2022, there were 19.54 million participants and 6.13 million contributors to the individual pension system, with a total amount of 14.2 billion yuan.	no

交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the R&D department of the bank said that the pilot-stage pension and personal pension products have three characteristics compared to other personal pension products.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is robustness, more robust risk management mechanisms, more robust investment strategies and philosophies, and the implementation of independent custody by non-parent third parties.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	The second is long-term, the pilot phase of the term of the pension plan is 5 years or more, the next step of the personal pension plan, the minimum holding period is in principle 1 year, encouraging holding more than 3 years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is the universality, the threshold for purchasing products is low, the starting point is generally 1 yuan, some are as low as 0.01 yuan, the cost of hosting, administration fees and other fees for products are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Experts point out that investors should choose based on the characteristics of the product and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Individual pension savings have long term, high interest rate, high security characteristics, suitable for people with low risk tolerance; Individual pension insurance products are heavily secured, more suitable for people who cannot bear the investment risk, can accept stable returns; and Individual pension property management products and public fund products are not secured and do not guarantee returns, there is some investment risk, but the expected return is high, suitable for people with a certain financial knowledge, risk tolerance.	no

南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	Nanjing property market to pay for the price difference - China News Network	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangon Evening News (Reporter Ma Zhongbo) Yangon Evening News / Zhuhai News reporter found in an interview on the 10th that the price guarantee agreement for the building, which has not been seen for more than ten years, has returned to the Nanjing real estate market. A property in Jiangbei New District claims that the price difference compensates for the building, and that the developer is willing to buy the house for the owner and refund the price difference.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	The price guarantee agreement has many conditions.	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	The property in Jiangbei New District is called the Bolian Zhongyuan Tai, and the owner, Mr. Sun, told reporters that he found a brick declaration when he was looking at the property last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The pictures he sent to reporters showed the developers of the property promising that if the preferential discount for other housing sources in the project is greater than the discount for previous purchases of housing for all housing sources purchased between February 1 and February 28, from the date of signing the purchase contract and until the delivery of the corresponding housing source, the developer can change the housing for the buyer and refund the difference in price.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Sun said that the real estate consultant said that this is actually a price guarantee agreement, the purpose is to make the buyer feel safe to go, without worrying about the development company's price reduction promotion, now that the price has been reduced, there is no time to go to the sales office, if not, it is really worrying.	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	Many buyers also believe that the price guarantee agreement is a good deal, even though it gives buyers a lot of money to settle their debts, but the conditions are not bad.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Liu, who is planning to buy a newly needed house in Jiangbei, said that the price of the house is first of all the same type of house, on the same floor, in the same unit, and the buyer can compare the price of the house with the price of the house, so the threshold is quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	Some buyers also believe that the information is asymmetrical, and that the sale does not exclude the possibility of an additional concession, which makes it difficult for the buyer to defend his rights.	yes
能否留住买房人有待观察	The question of whether to keep the buyer is still to be seen.	no
记者在南京网上房地产上查询得知，该楼盘于去年11月首领两幢楼共计252套房源的销许，户型面积有105平方米、114平方米、129平方米等，全装修销许均价为39843元/㎡。	The building was listed on the real estate website in November last year, with a total of 252 units in two floors, with a total area of 105 square meters, 114 square meters, 129 square meters, and a total of 39843 yuan / m2 for the average price of the fully renovated sale.	no
不过两个多月过去，网上房地产显示目前该楼盘的未售总套数为157套，占比为62.3%，其中8号楼共计128套，未售套数达113套，7号楼的124套中也有44套未售，项目的总成交套数只有33套，占比仅为13%。	However, over two months later, online real estate shows that the total number of unsold units in the complex is 157, accounting for 62.3%, of which 128 units are on the 8th floor, 113 units are unsold, 44 of the 124 units on the 7th floor are unsold, and the total number of completed units in the project is only 33, accounting for only 13%.	no
市场人士介绍，“保价协议”在2008年也曾在南京出现过。	The market sources said that the price guarantee agreement was also used in Nanjing in 2008.	no
当年8月份，河西黄山路上的楼盘横塘西苑为了吸引买房人眼球，推出了《保价计划》，具体内容为“公司郑重承诺，若一年内项目优惠幅度扩大，由此产生的差额，公司将按差额退还给老业主”。	In August of that year, in order to attract buyers, the company launched a price guarantee scheme, specifically promising the company that if the project's incentive margin expands within a year, the difference will be returned to the old owner.	no

报告：2022年回国求职留学生数量再创新高-中新网	Report: Number of international students returning to their home countries to seek jobs in 2022	yes
2022年回国求职应届留学生留学国前10 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	The top 10 countries for students to study abroad to find jobs in 2022	yes
中新网北京2月11日电 (门睿)近日发布的《2022中国海归就业调查报告》(下称“报告”)显示，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高，我国企业对海外人才的需求亦呈上扬态势。	The report of the China Expatriation Employment Survey (CES) for 2022 (hereinafter referred to as the "Expatriation Survey") released by Xinhua Beijing on February 11 (Minghui) shows that the number of international students returning to China for employment has increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the demand for overseas talent by Chinese enterprises has also increased.	yes
报告指出，自2020年以来，在中国国内求职的海归数量明显增长，回国求职的应届留学生数量增多。	The report notes that since 2020, the number of overseas students seeking jobs in China has increased significantly, and the number of overseas students returning to China to seek jobs has increased.	yes
与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	The number of international students returning to their home countries for work in 2022 is even higher, with an increase of 8.6% in the number of international students in 2022 compared to 2021.	yes
从回国求职留学生的留学国家分布来看，英国占比最高，为41.4%，其次是澳大利亚(20.3%)和美国(9%)，排名与2021年一致。	The UK has the highest proportion of students returning to study abroad for work, at 41.4%, followed by Australia (20.3%) and the US (9%), which is consistent with 2021.	yes
从同比增速来看，2022年来自马来西亚、日本、新加坡的应届留学生人数同比大幅上升，增速分别为66.1%、50.9%和37.7%。	In terms of year-on-year growth, the number of international students from Malaysia, Japan and Singapore will increase significantly in 2022 with a year-on-year growth of 66.1%, 50.9% and 37.7% respectively.	yes
来自加拿大、德国、美国、澳大利亚的应届留学生人数同比下降。	The number of international students from Canada, Germany, the United States and Australia decreased year-on-year.	yes
2023春节后第一周海归人才供需走势 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	The supply and demand of talent for the first week after the 2023 Spring Festival	yes
调研显示，决定回国的留学生中，58%认为“国内生活更加便利”，40%因“更认同国内的文化环境”决定回国，32%认为“国内就业机会更多”，22%认为国内经济活动会加速复苏，能获得更多就业机会。	The survey shows that 58% of the students who decided to return to their home country thought that they would have a better life in the country, 40% decided to return because they were more familiar with the cultural environment in the country, 32% thought that they would have more opportunities for employment in the country, and 22% thought that the recovery of the domestic economy would accelerate and provide more employment opportunities.	yes
数据显示，当前国内企业对海外人才的需求快速释放，对海归人才的需求呈上升趋势。	The data shows that the demand for overseas talent is rapidly unlocked by domestic companies, and the demand for repatriated talent is on the rise.	no
2023年春节后首周，海归优先的职位数和在国内求职的海归人数均呈上扬态势，2月3日的海归优先职位数比1月28日增长11%，海归求职人数增长27%。	In the first week after the Spring Festival 2023, the number of priority posts and the number of expatriates seeking jobs in the country rose, with the number of priority posts on February 3 increasing by 11% and the number of expatriate job seekers by 27% compared to January 28.	no
从行业看，2022年海归优先岗位中，来自教育/培训行业的职位数占比27.8%，位居第一位，专业服务/咨询、互联网/电子商务行业分别以14.3%、11.1%分列二三。	Education/training is the largest sector of the 2022 priority migration jobs, accounting for 27.8%, followed by professional services/consulting, Internet/e-commerce with 14.3% and 11.1% respectively.	no
近几年在国内求职的海归人数变化 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Changes in the number of expatriates seeking work in China in recent years	no
从薪酬看，海归优先职位的平均招聘薪酬连续三年走高，2022年达14680元/月(人民币，下同)，比2021年的13719元/月增加961元，增长7%。	The average recruitment salary for the priority positions in the country of origin has increased for three consecutive years, reaching 14,680 yuan/month in 2022 (in yuan, see below), an increase of 961 yuan/month from 13,719 yuan/month in 2021, an increase of 7% [2].	no
分地域看，2022年海归群体前往新一线城市、二线城市和三线及以下城市发展的意愿均有提升，2022年的投递占比分别为31%、15.7%和14.3%，均高于2021年的投递占比。	By geography, the willingness of the returnee group to travel to new tier 1, 2 and 3 cities and below has increased in 2022 with a delivery rate of 31%, 15.7% and 14.3% respectively, higher than the delivery rate in 2021.	no
对于留学的收获，52.7%的海归表示基本符合预期，相比上年(49.9%)提高了2.8个百分点。	For the study abroad, 52.7% of the returnees said that the return was mostly in line with expectations, an increase of 2.8 percentage points compared to the previous year (49.9%).	no

河南省规范整合口腔种植医疗服务价格-中新网	The price of integrated oral implantation services in Henan Province	yes
央视网消息：种植牙是很多缺牙患者的理想选择，但一直以来，动辄上万元一颗的价格让很多患者望而却步。	The idea of dental implants is an ideal option for many people with tooth loss, but the price of a tooth has been so high that many patients have been turned away.	yes
今年以来，随着种植牙集采的加速落地，各地也将种植牙降价提上日程。	This year, as the planting of the tooth is accelerating, the price reduction of the tooth will be added to the agenda.	yes
从2月10日起，河南省单颗常规种植牙医疗服务价格全流程调控目标为4300元，单颗常规种植全流程费用不高于调控目标的97%。	As of February 10, the price of a single conventional dental implantation in Henan Province is set at 4,300 yuan, and the cost of a single conventional implantation is not higher than 97% of the target.	yes
种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants are a form of dental restoration that support and fix the upper dentition by implanting lower structures within the bone tissue.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the University of Yangzhou First Affiliated Hospital that the price of a single conventional plant, from planting to final restoration, is about 167,000 yuan.	yes
患者 何莹：新政策之后，大夫跟我说，像我这种情况差不多就是8000多元、不到1万元，基本上能省一半。	Patient Hoon: After the new policy, my doctor told me that in my situation, it would be more than 8,000 yuan, less than 10,000 yuan, basically half of the savings.	yes
在现行项目基础上，河南省还整合确定了“种植体植入费(单颗)”等15个口腔种植类医疗服务价格项目，并统一制定省管公立医疗机构价格和医保支付类别，取消或调整了牙种植体植入术等20个医疗服务价格项目。	On the basis of the existing projects, Henan province also integrated the determination of 15 oral implantation medical service price projects such as the cost of gum implantation (single) gum, and unified the development of the price of provincial public health institutions and health insurance payment categories, and canceled or adjusted 20 medical service price projects such as dental implantation.	yes
郑州市医疗保障局医药价格和招标采购处处长 李云杰：受益的主要是四方，一个是医保，医保的支出少了；医院的占压少了，病人会适当增加；对供应商来说得到了一个市场；对我们患者来说是得利最大的一方，植一颗牙的费用可能要减半甚至更多。	Li Yunjie, Director of the Department of Drug Price and Tender Procurement of Zhengzhou City Health Insurance Bureau: The main benefits are four, one is health insurance, the cost of health insurance is less; the hospital is less occupied, the patient will increase appropriately; a market for suppliers is obtained; the biggest benefit for our patients is that the cost of a tooth transplant may be reduced by half or more.	yes

《计划》要求，全面提升5G网络能效。	The plan calls for a comprehensive upgrade of the 5G network's energy efficiency.	yes

支持基础电信企业加大对重点区域、场所5G网络的优化力度，全年新增5G基站10000个，全市平均下载速率达到500Mbps、上行速率达到100Mbps，重点区域下载速率达到1000Mbps、上行速率达到200Mbps，网络速率和用户体验感大幅提升。	Supporting basic telecommunications companies to increase the optimization of 5G networks in key areas and locations, adding 10,000 new 5G base stations throughout the year, reaching an average download rate of 500Mbps, upstream rate of 100Mbps, download rate of 1000Mbps in key areas, upstream rate of 200Mbps, and significantly improving network speed and user experience.	yes
打造城市级高品质无线局域网。	The project is aimed at building a high-quality, urban-grade wireless LAN.	yes
制定公共场所无线局域网(WLAN)服务规范，推动全市各区人员密集和信息消费需求集中区域WLAN升级，提供千兆接入能力。	Develop WLAN service specifications for public places, and promote the upgrading of WLANs in areas with high population density and information consumption needs in all districts of the city, providing gigabit access capabilities.	yes

报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	The report argues that the content ecology of the e-commerce industry is a comprehensive concept, which is to integrate e-commerce with content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce, good PGC (professional production content) and UGC (user original content) is the quality of the integration with e-commerce carriers, the higher the value of the content platform, the more abundant the consumption and promotion of the scene, the greater the possibility of e-commerce implantation, the stronger the commercial value, the higher the proportion of e-commerce content production and content consumption of this gradual integration of components in the public and private sectors.	no

（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	The Biden administration on Friday blacklisted six Chinese entities suspected of involvement in the balloon spy program.	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The US Commerce Department said the five Chinese companies and one research institute helped modernize the Chinese military, especially its aerospace programs, including its aircraft carriers and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	The blacklisted companies have a hard time getting their technology exported to the US.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is called the Entity List, and companies on it will not be able to buy technology or goods from U.S. suppliers unless they obtain a special export license from the U.S. Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The companies included in the blacklist are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., the 48th Institute of China Electronics and Technology Group, Dongguan Liangqiang Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Xiamen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Tianhai Xiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd. and Shanxi Xiamen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	Before that, the White House said it was considering broader measures to expose and deal with the larger scale of Chinese surveillance that threatens US national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident has further heightened tensions between China and the United States, with US Secretary of State Blinken cancelling a planned visit to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	The Chinese government has criticized the US for its heavy interference in the US embassy in China, which was hit by the US air strike on February 4, and for the damage it has caused to the efforts and processes of stabilizing China-US relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	Based on the evidence of the wreckage and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the US government concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon had a direct relationship with the People's Liberation Army of China and was a supplier approved by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Mao Ning said at a press conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained its position on the accidental entry of a Chinese unmanned aircraft into US airspace due to force majeure.	yes
根据外交部网站，她补充表示，美国国会的有关决议案纯属政治操弄和炒作。	According to the Foreign Ministry website, she added that the relevant resolution of the US Congress is a pure political manipulation and a hoax.	no
中方对此强烈不满、坚决反对。	The Chinese side strongly disagrees and strongly opposes this.	no

（德国之声中文网）距离土耳其和叙利亚部分地区发生地震已经过去数日，找到幸存者的希望日渐渺茫，然而在周六获救的一家五口却令搜救人员感到无比欣慰。	The hope of finding survivors has been fading for days after the earthquake hit parts of Turkey and Syria, but the relief of the rescuers on Saturday was the rescue of five people.	yes
据美联社报道，在加济安泰普省的重灾区努尔达伊镇，这个五口之家在废墟之下受困五天多之后，被成功营救。	The five-member family was rescued from the rubble in the town of Nurdai, in the heavily affected province of Gaziantep, after being trapped under the rubble for more than five days, according to the Associated Press.	yes
搜救人员先是从一堆废墟中拉出了母亲和女儿，随后找到了父亲，但他坚持要求先救自己的儿子和另一个女儿。	Rescuers pulled the mother and daughter from the rubble and then found the father, but he insisted on saving his son and another daughter first.	yes
当他们全部获救之后，人群中响起了欢呼声。	When they were all rescued, the crowd shouted for joy.	yes

与此同时，救援工作的重点开始转向帮助那些急需救助的幸存者。	Meanwhile, the focus of the rescue effort has shifted to helping survivors who are in dire need of help.	no

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	Chile earthquake of 1960	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 pm local time on May 22, 1960, the largest earthquake ever recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile, with a magnitude of 9.5 on the Richter scale.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	In just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was reduced to rubble.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami that hit the Chilean coastline, raising waves as high as 25 meters.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami reached as far as Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of people killed and the economic damage caused by such a catastrophe is unknown.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	The Great Alaska Earthquake of 1964 is a notable example of this phenomenon.	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 was a Friday, and it was also the day of the Passion of Jesus.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	The largest earthquake in North American history, measuring 9.2 on the Richter scale, occurred on this day in Alaska, USA.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	The Alaska earthquake was the third largest earthquake on record until 2006.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	A fault between the Pacific Plate and the North American Plate broke at Prince William Bay near College Cove during the earthquake.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	The earthquake lasted for 3 to 5 minutes in most areas.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	The sea floor shifted and triggered a huge tsunami, 67 meters high.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Schools and many businesses were closed as it was a holiday.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake killed 139 people.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Nine of them died directly from the earthquake, and another 130 died from the tsunami caused by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	The 1976 Tangshan earthquake	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two earthquakes of magnitude 7 or above occurred in 16 hours in Tangshan City and Funan County, Hebei Province, China.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The quake was centered 23 kilometers above the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	The city of Tangshan was completely destroyed, with all traffic, communications, water and electricity cut off.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	The strongest tremors were felt in Beijing, the capital, 140 kilometers away.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, the earthquake killed 242,769 people and seriously injured 164,851 people in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake was the second deadliest earthquake in recorded history in China, after the Great Quetzalcoatl Earthquake of 1556.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	But overseas scientists estimate that the earthquake may have killed at least 650,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	The Indian Ocean earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On 26 December 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 km off the western coast of Aceh, Sumatra, Indonesia, with a magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3 at a depth of 30 km.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with waves ranging from 15 to 30 meters high.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	The worst affected areas include the Indonesian province of Indochina, Thailand's Penang and Phuket resort areas, Sri Lanka and the Indian state of Tamil Nadu.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	The quake was a major natural disaster that occurred in the area of the city of New York, in the summer of 2011 and caused a massive influx of tourists and locals, which led to many tourists who were on holiday on the beach and locals who worked on the beach being swept away by the tsunami, leaving many people missing.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	The death toll and the number of missing persons is estimated to be at least 300,000.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake to hit the world in 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	The 2008 Wenchuan earthquake	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	A major earthquake occurred in the Wenchuan area of Sichuan Province, China on May 12, 2008.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to the China Earthquake Bureau, the quake had a magnitude of 8.2 and a magnitude of 8.3, with an area of more than 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, the earthquake has killed 69,227 people, left 17,923 missing, injured 374,643 people of varying degrees, and left 330,000 people homeless, with a total population of 4,625,600.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China, and the deadliest since the Great Tangshan Earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, the State Council announced that May 12 would be designated as National Day for Disaster Prevention and Mitigation, to increase public education and awareness of disaster prevention and mitigation.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	Since then, many Chinese governments and primary and secondary schools have held earthquake drills on this day every year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	The school has also started to emphasize the importance of earthquake and disaster prevention education.	no

海地地震（2010年）	The 2010 Haiti earthquake	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, a magnitude 7.0 earthquake occurred in the Caribbean island nation of Haiti.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter was located 25 kilometers southwest of the capital, Port-au-Prince, and about 13 kilometers above the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Committee of the Red Cross estimates that about 3 million people were affected by the earthquake.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The Haitian government has announced that the confirmed death toll is over 200,000.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some parts of Haiti, up to 90% of the houses were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Despite the massive aid and support from the international community, the overpopulated and corrupt poor country has never recovered from the disaster.	no

日本东北大地震（2011年）	The Great Northeast Japan Earthquake of 2011	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	A magnitude 9.0 earthquake struck off the northeast coast of Japan on March 11, 2011.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture. The epicenter was measured at a depth of 24 kilometers and triggered a huge tsunami that reached a maximum height of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	The earthquake was the first earthquake to exceed a magnitude of 9 since Japan's record-keeping began.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	Some 22,000 people were killed in the disaster, and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi nuclear power plant was affected by the tsunami and the leakage.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	The accident was classified as the 7th worst in the International Nuclear Event Classification (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	The Fukushima nuclear accident led to measurements of trace radioactive material worldwide, including uranium-131, uranium-137 (with a half-life of 30 years).	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	The accident released a large amount of radioactive isotopes into the Pacific Ocean.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to the United Nations, at least 870,000 people are in dire need of food in the Syrian-Turkish conflict zone.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, up to 5.3 million people were displaced by the earthquake.	no
世界粮食计划署（WFP）呼吁拨款7700万美元，为土耳其和叙利亚因为地震而流离失所的灾民提供食物。	The World Food Programme (WFP) is appealing for $77 million to provide food to people displaced by the earthquake in Turkey and Syria.	no
目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	The weather is now below freezing and many people are homeless.	no
土耳其政府分发了大量的热餐、帐篷和毯子，但是这些物资仍然难以送达很多急需帮助的人。	The Turkish government has distributed a large number of hot meals, tents and blankets, but these supplies are still difficult to get to the many people in need.	no
而在深陷内战泥潭长达12年之久的叙利亚，地震则使民众的苦难处境雪上加霜。	In Syria, which has been in the throes of a civil war for 12 years, the earthquake has added to the suffering of the people.	no
在地震发生后的四天内，世界粮食计划署已经向土耳其和叙利亚的11.5万人提供了食物救济。	In the four days after the earthquake, the World Food Programme (WFP) has provided food assistance to 115,000 people in Turkey and Syria.	no
世界卫生组织（WHO）则送去了72吨用于外伤处理和紧急手术的医药物资。	The World Health Organization (WHO) has sent 72 tons of medical supplies for trauma and emergency surgery.	no

NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: Police department calls for public to beware of fake SMS scam by fake telecom companies	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	The police recently discovered a number of cases of fraudulent telecommunications, where criminals have faked the company to send fraudulent SMS with a link to the website to the owner, in order to get the points to be exchanged as soon as possible, and to entice the fraudster to log into the fake website for exchange.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The clerk entered the credit card information and verification code as instructed, and immediately received a notification from the financial institution that the credit card had an unknown consumption record, suspecting that the credit card information had been stolen from the above-mentioned website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	The message was not sent by the telecommunications company.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The Sheriff's Office calls on citizens to be vigilant when receiving such text messages, not to log on to the website linking to the text message or provide any personal information, and to be extra cautious when asked to provide credit card information, account transaction passwords, transaction verification codes, and to prevent credit card theft.	yes
防骗提示：	Tips to prevent fraud:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Increased attention to cybersecurity information and awareness of personal security;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Avoid random access to unknown websites and register personal and credit card information on the websites to avoid theft;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be alert to fake and phishing websites and ensure that the URLs of the websites are in full agreement with the official websites;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software on mobile phones, mobile devices or computers and update it regularly;	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. In case of suspicion of fraud or other crime, the police department should immediately call the Fraud Prevention Hotline 8800 7777 or the Crime Reporting Hotline 993.	no

新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore tourism recovery strong, inbound travelers up 19x from 2021	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	The Singapore Tourism Board recently announced that 12 to 14 million international visitors are expected to visit Singapore in 2023, bringing about 18 to 21 billion yuan in tourism revenue; visitor numbers and tourism revenue will return to about 67 to 75 percent of pre-coronavirus levels in 2019; and there is a strong possibility of a full recovery in the tourism industry in 2024.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	Singapore Tourism Market to be restarted and revived in 2022	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	The latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board show that inbound visitors in 2022 will increase 19-fold from 33.06 million in 2021 to 6.3 million, exceeding the previous estimate of 4 to 6 million, and returning to 33 percent of pre-pandemic levels.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	Singapore's tourism revenue totaled S$8.96 billion in January-September 2022, and is expected to reach S$13.8 billion to S$14.3 billion in full-year 2022, up six to seven times from S$1.89 billion in 2021, and has recovered to levels of about 50 to 52 percent of pre-coronavirus levels in 2019.	yes
新加坡政府多措并举，加速旅游业复苏。	The Singapore government has taken several steps to speed up the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes

旅游局日前宣布，将计划在未来两年从这笔预算中拨出1.1亿新元，推出更多商业和休闲活动吸引旅客回流。	The Tourism Board recently announced that it plans to allocate 110 million yuan from the budget over the next two years to launch more commercial and leisure activities to attract returning tourists.	yes

Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: How do you see the January non-farm employment data in the US exceeding expectations and future trends?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: January 3, 2023 nonfarm employment data released by the U.S. Department of Labor, adding 517,000 nonfarm jobs, significantly higher than the market expectation of 189,000; unemployment rate dropped to 3.4%, the lowest level in nearly 50 years; hourly wage growth was 4.4%, year-over-year growth was 0.3%, slightly slower.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	In total, there are many one-time and technical factors that have disrupted the data, such as teachers who are on strike, the revision of the survey caliber, the update of the seasonality factor, which may be corrected later (refer to the new non-agricultural increase in January 2022 from 504,000 to 364,000), and non-agricultural employment may not be as strong as the data shows.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	Structurally, the impact of high-tech firms' layoffs remains, but is low; new jobs in high-touch services such as leisure hotels, education and healthcare have recovered significantly, and data shows that the service sector's labor force gap remains.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combined with the equally over-expected service PMI, the rebound in job vacancies and the labor gap data, and the strength of consumer credit data, we judge that the US service sector is in a fast recovery after the extreme weather and the holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	We believe that the supply and demand tensions in the US job market will not improve without a recession.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	The U.S. labor market is still short of more than 5 million workers, and labor participation is slowly increasing, especially among those aged 25-54 who are nearing their pre-pandemic highs.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition, strong consumer demand, due to the strength of excess savings and consumer credit of US residents, will further delay the impact of austerity policies on the labor market.	yes
美国就业市场供需持续紧张将是2023年美国经济的底色。	The continued tension in the US labor market will be the underlying cause of the US economy in 2023.	yes
