本次数据公布前，美国股债汇市场对于美联储加息路径的预期过于乐观。	Prior to the data, the US equity and debt markets were overly optimistic about the Fed's path to raising interest rates.	no
随着通胀数据的持续改善，美联储在缩短加息步伐的同时还不断维系着市场通胀预期脆弱的平衡，但市场对于美联储偏向鹰派的表述视而不见，不仅预期提前停止加息，还预期年末两次降息。	With the continuing improvement in inflation data, the Fed is slowing down the pace of rate hikes and maintaining the fragile balance of market inflation expectations, but the market is blind to the Fed's biased narratives, not only expecting an early end to the rate hike, but also expecting two rate cuts by the end of the year.	no
在劳动力市场供需紧张，紧缩政策影响不明的情况下，我们认为美联储年末对于加息的指引是相对合理的，市场极端预期的调整和交易的拥挤或将对市场产生一定伤害。	In a situation of tight supply and demand in the labor market and uncertain impact of austerity policy, we believe that the guidance of the US Federal Reserve for raising interest rates at the end of the year is relatively reasonable, and the extreme adjustment and crowding of transactions expected in the market will cause some damage to the market.	no
尽管如此，薪资增速的顽固难改当前通胀快速下降的趋势，随着M2数据同比转负以及各个CPI分项领先指标的逐渐转好，自10月份以来美国CPI数据已经转向快速下降阶段，薪资增速的顽固仅会对以后的通胀数据形成托底，当前的市场预期难以证伪，在下一期通胀数据公布后市场或进入新一轮博弈。	However, the persistence of wage growth is difficult to change the current trend of rapidly declining inflation, with the M2 data year-on-year overload and the gradual improvement of the leading indicators of various CPI sub-indices, since October, the US CPI data has moved into a phase of rapid decline, the persistence of wage growth will only form the basis for future inflation data, the current market expectations are difficult to falsify, after the next inflation data is released, the market will enter a new round of games.	no
杉杉创始人郑永刚因突发心脏疾病过世 曾带领中国服装第一股转型 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	The founder of Suzuki, Yang Yonggang, died of a sudden heart attack after leading the first transformation of Chinese clothing - Economic Watch Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes

(hereinafter referred to as Sugiyama Holding Co., Ltd.) that the founder of Sugiyama Enterprises, Chairman of the Board of Directors of Sugiyama Holding Co., Ltd., Yang Yongkang, died on February 10, 2023 at the age of 65 due to sudden cardiac arrest.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 1980s, Yang was the head of the state-owned cotton mill, and in 1989 he became the head of the Ningbo Yun Port General Clothing Factory, the predecessor of the Sugyu Group.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, during the 20th Annual Meeting of Chinese Business Leaders and the 22nd Annual Meeting of the Future Star of Chinese Enterprises, Yang Yonggang said that in the 1990s, the market share of the Sugu brand in the Chinese western clothing market was as high as 37%.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Sugihisawa became the first company in the Chinese clothing industry to list its shares on the stock exchange.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just as the clothing business was booming, the Sugiyashi Group began to transform, because Yang Yonggang realized that once the market opened, Chinese brands would naturally form a tiered brand market, and Sugiyashi clothing wanted to be the only one to dominate the hype, and it was unlikely to become the national clothing of the country for a long time.	yes
1999年，杉杉开始研究企业转型，郑永刚回忆当年 ， “ 我们来到上海，寻求到底转型做什么，专门找了很多专家学者，连续不断地开一些诸葛亮会、务虚研讨会。	In 1999, Sugisugi started to study corporate transformation, and Yang Yonggang recalled that year, "We came to Shanghai to find out what transformation really does, and we specifically sought out many expert scholars, and we held a series of discussions and workshops".	yes
最后，我们设定了两个大的战略方向。	Finally, we have set two major strategic directions:	yes
第一个方向是新能源新材料，另外一个是大健康有未来 ” 。	The first is new energy and new materials, the other is a healthy future.	yes
战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Sugiyama began to look for cooperation. At that time, the Carbon Institute of the Busan Institute of Thermal Energy was doing the national 863 project for the aluminum steel, and the scientific funding was not enough.	yes

因为大家都会去考虑，我花了那么多钱，我得去派人管对吧，这是通常会做的一个行为 ” ， 然而郑永刚则不同，杉杉收购成功的那一天，郑永刚就到杉金光电当众宣布，杉杉作为杉金的大股东，决定实施一企两制，除了郑永刚担任董事长，杉杉企业的人不派到杉金，采取授权经营的方式，原有的分配制度、企业文化、各项管理等模式不变。	But it's different with Yang Yonggang, because the day that the acquisition was successful, Yang Yonggang went to Seagate and announced to the public that Seagate, as the major shareholder of Seagate, had decided to implement the one-two system, except for Yang Yonggang as chairman, the people of Seagate's enterprise were not sent to Seagate, and the authorized way of operating, the original distribution system, corporate culture, and management models were unchanged.	no

据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	The E-account of the fund provides individual investors with one-stop-shop information on the account and shares of the fund, which is aimed at solving the pain points of the industry such as the forgotten accounts of large and small investors, and the burdensome queries.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, as of the end of 2022, there were 156 ETF managers in the country, managing funds of about 26 trillion yuan; 167 ETF share registration agencies, and 411 ETF sales agencies.	yes

“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the E-account app?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to the documents, the E-Account App is a Chinese-developed and approved by the China Securities Regulatory Commission to provide investors with a one-stop query of the off-site holdings of shares in the entire market of E-Funds products.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Investors can easily and quickly access their ownership of the OTC shares of the fund managers' OTC products purchased through the various sales channels in the market through the OTC E account, which improves the overall efficiency of queries.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can access through the E-account window of the E-fund includes: information about fund accounts opened with various E-fund managers in the market, information about trading accounts opened with E-fund sales agencies, and information about the number of investors holding off-site shares in products such as the open-ended securities investment fund and the collective asset management plan established by the management of the securities company, which is not limited to 200 people.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	The Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation Research Center Business Manager Liu Yiqi told Economic Observer that investors can learn all their OTC fund holdings through the OTC fund E account app, which helps them find forgotten asset classes, and more importantly, the full account information of the integrated fund investment situation has been compiled for customers, helping customers to better optimize their fund portfolio configuration and better plan their financial arrangements.	no

值得注意的是，“基金E账户”仅为投资者提供查询服务，并不能进行申赎买卖。	It is worth noting that the E-account window of the Hedge Fund only provides an inquiry service for investors and does not allow for redemption.	no
“基金 E 账户”所显示的数据日期一般为用户进行查询的日期（T日)往前推三个交易日。	The data date shown in the E account window of the hedge fund is generally three trading days forward of the date of the user's query (T-day).	no
比如，在2 月10日打开“基金E账户”，资产页所显示的总资产、基金份额、基金净值对应日期为该日期往前推三个交易日，即2月7日。	For example, if the E account of a hedge fund is opened on February 10, the total assets, fund shares, and net worth of the fund shown on the asset page are moved forward three trading days from that date, i.e., February 7.	no

东德最后一位共产党总理今去世	The last Communist Chancellor of East Germany died today.	yes
东德共产党的继任者在该党在一份声明中报告，“昨晚，汉斯·莫德罗 (Hans Modrow) 离开了我们，享年 95 岁。	The successor to the East German Communist Party reported in a statement that Hans Modrow passed away last night at the age of 95.	yes
因此，我们的党失去了一位重要领导人。	As a result, our party lost an important leader.	yes
”	The Crab	yes
1989 年 11 月 13 日，在将东柏林和西柏林分开 28 年的柏林墙打开四天后，莫德罗曾表示他将帮助把东德变成一个民主国家。	On November 13, 1989, four days after the opening of the Berlin Wall, which had separated East and West Berlin for 28 years, Moderator said he would help transform East Germany into a democratic state.	yes
当时，由于东德各地的抗议者要求民主和自由，共产党领导人被迫下台。	The Communist Party leaders were forced to step down as protesters across East Germany demanded democracy and freedom.	yes
戈尔巴乔夫 (Mikhail Gorbachev) 在苏联上台后曾要求在苏联主导的东欧也进行变革。	After Mikhail Gorbachev came to power in the Soviet Union, he called for changes in Soviet-dominated Eastern Europe as well.	yes
1990 年 3 月，莫德罗宣布德意志民主共和国 (GDR) 的第一次也是唯一一次自由选举。	In March 1990, Modrow declared the first and only free elections in the German Democratic Republic (GDR).	yes
选举结果导致他不再担任总理。	The election results have made him no longer the Prime Minister.	yes
尽管莫德罗进行了改革，但反对者指责他试图推迟 1990 年 10 月发生的政治变革和统一。	Despite Modro's reforms, opponents accuse him of trying to delay the political change and unification that took place in October 1990.	yes
他还因试图重塑而不是废除秘密警察而受到批评。	He has also been criticized for trying to reform rather than abolish the secret police.	no
1993 年，莫德罗在 1989 年 5 月的市政选举中被判选举舞弊罪名成立，但并未入狱。	In 1993, Modro was convicted of electoral fraud in the May 1989 municipal elections, but was not jailed.	no
有称这些指控是出于政治动机。	The accusations are politically motivated.	no
1990 年至 1994 年，莫德罗继续在德国议会任职，并于 1999 年至 2004 年担任欧洲议会议员。	Modrow continued to serve in the German parliament from 1990 to 1994, and was a member of the European Parliament from 1999 to 2004.	no
莫德罗将自己视为一名改革者，并希望从内部改变共产党。	Modro sees himself as a reformer and wants to change the Communist Party from within.	no
1999 年，他告诉路透社，他不希望旧东德回归，但表示应该承认东德的成就。	In 1999, he told Reuters that he did not want the old East Germany to return, but that East Germany's achievements should be recognized.	no
莫德罗于 1928 年出生在当时的德国小镇 Jasenitz（现为波兰的 Jasienica），并接受过机械师培训。	Modrow was born in 1928 in the then German town of Jasenitz (now Jasienica, Poland) and trained as a mechanic.	no
第二次世界大战期间，他担任青年消防队排长，并在冲突快结束时成为纳粹民兵组织 Volkssturm 的一员，该组织征召 16 至 60 岁的男子参加最后的战争挣扎。	During World War II he served as a youth fire brigade commander and became a member of the Volkssturm, a Nazi militia organization that recruited men between the ages of 16 and 60 to participate in the final struggle of the war, near the end of the conflict.	no
17 岁时，莫德罗被苏联军队俘虏，作为战俘被带到苏联，在那里他参加了反法西斯课程，并成为一名坚定的共产党员。	At the age of 17, Modrow was captured by the Soviet army and taken to the Soviet Union as a prisoner of war, where he took anti-fascist courses and became a committed Communist Party member.	no
1949 年，即东德成立的那一年，他回国后找到了一份机械师的工作，并继续学习社会科学和经济学，并获得了博士学位。	In 1949, the year of the founding of East Germany, he returned to his homeland and found a job as a mechanic, and continued his studies in social sciences and economics, obtaining a doctorate.	no
莫德罗是自由德国青年运动的一名工作人员，几乎所有东德年轻人都加入了该运动，并在 1973 年至 1989 年期间通过执政的社会统一党 (SED) 晋升为德累斯顿地区党的主席。	Modrow was a staff member of the Free German Youth movement, which almost all East German youth joined, and was promoted through the ruling Socialist Unity Party (SED) to chairman of the Dresden regional party from 1973 to 1989.	no
他还在东德任职议会超过 30 年。	He also served in the East German parliament for over 30 years.	no
1990 年莫德罗成为东德事实上的领导人，担任最高国家职务。	In 1990, Modrow became de facto leader of East Germany, holding the highest state office.	no

扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	They are lost in their own vain imaginations.	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	The US military used its most advanced stealth fighter aircraft, the F-22, to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska, USA, on Friday afternoon.	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The site of the crash is ten miles off the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the US military has shot down an object in the air.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	On Saturday, a spy balloon from China was shot down over the coast of South Carolina, USA, days after it drifted in US airspace.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The second object shot down, which first entered U.S. airspace on Thursday night, was tracked by the U.S. military as it moved over northeastern Alaska, at an altitude of 12,000 meters (~40,000 feet), the size of a small car, and much smaller than the Chinese balloon that was shot down earlier, the Pentagon said.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is no indication that the object is manoeuvrable.	yes
